==== Odyssee 4 ====
(1) οἱ(Pr)(N) δʼ(Pt) ἷξον(AorS)(Akt) κοίλην(Adj)(A) Λακεδαίμονα(A) κητώεσσαν(Adj)(A),
(1) sie aber kamen hohl Lakedaímon schlucht|reich,
(1) they but came hollow Lacedaemon full|of|sea|monsters,
(2) πρὸς(Prp) δʼ(Pt) ἄρα(Pt) δώματʼ(A) ἔλων(AorS)(Akt) Μενελάου(G) κυδαλίμοιο(Adj)(G).
(2) zu aber nun Häuser nahmen des|Menelaos ruhm|reichen.
(2) toward but then halls went of|Menelaos glorious.
(3) τὸν(Pr)(A) δʼ(Pt) εὗρον(AorS)(Akt) δαινύντα(Prä)(Akt)(A) γάμον(A) πολλοῖσιν(Adj)(D) ἔτῃσιν(D)
(3) den aber fanden feiernd Hochzeit vielen Jahren
(3) him but found feasting wedding in|many years
(4) υἱέος(G) ἠδὲ(Kon) θυγατρὸς(G) ἀμύμονος(Adj)(G) ᾧ(Pr)(D) ἐνὶ(Prp) οἴκῳ(D).
(4) des|Sohnes und der|Tochter tadellosen welchem in Hause.
(4) of|a|son and of|a|daughter blameless which in house.

(5) die zwar des|Achilleus Reihen|brech|ers dem|Sohn sandte·
(5) her indeed of|Achilles breaker|of|ranks to|the|son was|sending·

(6) in Troja denn zuerst versprach und nickte|zu
(6) in Troy for at|first promised and nodded

(7) to|give, to|them but gods marriage were|completing.

(8) her then he indeed there with|horses and with|chariots sent to|return

(9) of|the|Myrmidons toward city very|famous, over|whom ruled.

(10) for|the|son but from|Sparta of|Alector was|taking maiden,
